		<script>
	// Depeding on page - set parameters for DFP
	(function(){
		var pg = window.pageName2 || window.pageName ;
		//Array to store all ads
		var arr728 = [],arr200=[];
		switch(pg){
			case 'productDeals' : 
				arr728.push({sel : ".breadsearch-row", rev : 1 ,css : 'text-align: center; margin: 20px 0 0 0;' });
				arr728.push({sel : "#dfp-div-2", rev : -1 , type : 2 });
				arr728.push({sel : "#thenewGoogleDfpId", rev : -1 , id : "thenewGoogleDfpId"});
				arr728.push({sel : "#dfp-div-3", rev : -1 });
			break;
			case 'search' :
				arr728.push({sel : ".searchResult-text-wrapper", rev : 1 ,css : 'padding : 0 0 10px 0;' });
			case 'pdp' :
				arr728.push({sel : ".pdp_dfp > *:eq(0)", rev : 1,type : 2 ,css : 'padding : 0 0 10px 16px;' });
			break;
			case 'csf' : 
				arr728.push({sel : ".breadsearch-row", rev : 1 ,css : 'text-align: center; margin : 20px 0 0 0;' });
				//window.isBelowSlideShow = "false" == "true";
			break;
			case 'brandPage' :
			case 'brandCategoryPage':
				arr728.push({sel : ".brand-head-box:eq(0)", rev : 1 ,css : 'padding : 0 0 10px 0;' });
				arr728.push({sel : "#thenewGoogleDfpId", rev : -1 , id : "thenewGoogleDfpId"});
			break;
		};
		var a728Arr = [] , a200Arr = [];
		var ids = 0 ;
		// Add slots in required places
		for (var i = 0 ; i < arr728.length ; i++){
			var item = arr728[i];
			if(!item)
				continue;
			var it = item.sel;
			var rev = item.rev || false ;
			if(rev == -1) {
				// use the same
				var id = $(it).attr('id') || item.id;
				if(id){
					if(item.type == 2){
						a200Arr.push(id);			 
					} else {
						a728Arr.push(id);
					}
				}
				continue;
			}
			var id = 'dfp728-'+(ids++);
			if(item.type == 2){
				a200Arr.push(id);			 
			} else {
				a728Arr.push(id);
			}
			var itemClass = item.cssClass || "" , itemStyle = item.css || "" ;
			var divStr = "<div style='"+itemStyle+"' class='"+itemClass+"' id='"+id+"'></div>";
			switch(rev){			
				case 1 : $(divStr).insertBefore(it).hide();
				break;
				case 0 : $(it).append(divStr);
				break;
				default : $(divStr).insertAfter(it);
			}
		}				
		window.a728Arr = a728Arr , window.a200Arr = a200Arr ;
	})();
</script>
<script async type="text/javascript" src="http://www.googletagservices.com/tag/js/gpt.js"></script>
	<script type='text/javascript'>
			var counter = 0 ;
			var pref = 'Ad_Unit_';
	function triggerGoogleDfp(counter){
			counter = counter || window.counter; 
			var arr728 = window.a728Arr ,
				arr200 =  window.a200Arr , 
				dfpuser = "129473952" ,
				dpfcurl = unescapeHtml("mobiles") , pagename = window.pageName;
			
			for (var i = 0 ; i < arr728.length ; i++){
				var it = arr728[i];
				if(counter >= 1)
					counter = 1;	
				window.topBannerDfp = googletag.defineSlot('/'+dfpuser+'/728x90_'+pref+(counter+1), [728, 90], it).setCollapseEmptyDiv(true, true);
				counter = 1;
				if(window.topBannerDfp)
					window.topBannerDfp.addService(googletag.pubads());
			}
			for (var i = 0 ; i < arr200.length ; i++){
				var it = arr200[i];
				var obj1 = googletag.defineSlot('/'+dfpuser+'/200x200_'+pref+(i+2), [200, 200], it).setCollapseEmptyDiv(true, true);
  				if(obj1)
					obj1.addService(googletag.pubads());
			}
			googletag.pubads().enableSingleRequest();
			googletag.pubads().collapseEmptyDivs();
			googletag.pubads().setTargeting('category',dpfcurl);
			if(window.brandName){
				googletag.pubads().setTargeting('brand',window.brandName);
			}
			//googletag.pubads().setTargeting('brand',dpfcurl);
			googletag.pubads().setTargeting('pagetype',pagename);
			googletag.enableServices();
			
			for (var i = 0 ; i < arr728.length ; i++){
				var it = arr728[i];
				googletag.display(it); 
			}
			for (var i = 0 ; i < arr200.length ; i++){
				var it = arr200[i];
				googletag.display(it); 
			}
			arr728.length = 0 ; arr200.length = 0 ;
			googletag.pubads().refresh(window.topBannerDfp);
		};
	var googletag = googletag || {};
	googletag.cmd = googletag.cmd || [];
	googletag.cmd.push(function() {
		triggerGoogleDfp();
	});
	</script>

<script src="http://www.google.com/adsense/search/ads.js" type="text/javascript"></script> 
	<script type="text/javascript">
		function triggerGoogleAdsense(){
			var queryContext = $('a[catId="'+$('#categoryId').val() + '"]').attr('name');
			queryContext = queryContext || "";
			
			function getNumberOfAds(numAdsMap) {
		      	for(var name  in numAdsMap) {
		      		if(numAdsMap[name] == '0') {
		      			$('#' + name + "-div").hide();
		      		}
		      	}
		    }
			
			var pageOptions = { 
			  'pubId': AdSenseOpt.pubId ,
			  'query': AdSenseOpt.query,
			  'hl': 'en',
			  'adtest': 'off',
			  'linkTarget' : '_blank',
			  'queryContext' : AdSenseOpt.queryContext,
			  'channel' : 'searchBin',
			  'noTitleUnderline': false,
			  'adsResponseCallback': getNumberOfAds,
			  'location': false,
			  'plusOnes': false,
			  'sellerRatings': false,
			  'siteLinks': false
			};
			
			var adblock1 = { 
			  'container': 'google-ads',
			  'number': '3',
			  'width': '220px',		  
			  'lines': '1',
			  'fontFamily': 'tahoma',
			  'fontSizeTitle': '14px',
			  'fontSizeDescription': '12px',
			  'fontSizeDomainLink': '12px',
			  'colorTitleLink': '004B91',
			  'colorText': '828282',
			  'colorDomainLink': 'A0A09E'
			};
			var args = [];
			args.push(pageOptions);
			var  adopts = window.adopts ;
			for (var i = 0 ; i < adopts.length ; i++  ){
				var adSenseoptions = adopts[i];
				var clone = $.extend({},adblock1);
				var block = $.extend(clone,adSenseoptions);
				if($('#'+block.container).length > 0 )
					args.push(block);
			}
			// For Variable args to 'new' constructor 
			function construct(constructor, args) {
			    function F() {
			        return constructor.apply(this, args);
			    }
			    F.prototype = constructor.prototype;
			    return new F();
			}
	
			try {	
				construct(google.ads.search.Ads ,args);
			} catch (err) {
				console.log(err);
		//		$('#google-ads-div').hide();
			}
		}
		$(window).load(function(){
			try{
				triggerGoogleAdsense();
			}catch(e){console.log(e);};
		});
	</script>
